                limit = { has_active_mission=workers_entering_factories }

                set_temp_variable={ tmpDIS=30 }

country_event = {
	id = hellas.2
	title = hellas.2.t
	desc = hellas.2.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_gre_metaxas

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

    immediate={
        hidden_effect={
            clear_variable=emergency_powers_cost
            add_stability=0.20
            add_war_support=0.25
            swap_ruler_traits = { remove = greek_dictator add = arkhigos_0 }
            complete_national_focus = GRE_the_4th_of_august_regime
            set_party_name = {
                ideology = neutrality
                long_name = "Kathestós tis 4hs Augoústou"
                name = "4h Augoústou"
            }
            set_country_flag = GRE_kathestos_proclaimed
            GRE_ioannis_metaxas = { vscope_from_cscope=yes cscope_increase_title=yes }
            GRE_kostas_kotzias = { vscope_from_cscope=yes cscope_increase_title=yes }
            set_variable = { GRE_ark = 0 }
            if = { 
                limit = { check_variable = { decision_taken = 0 } } 
                custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_papagos_selection_tt
                ###[ FACTION MECHANICS ]###
                if={
                    limit={ has_country_flag=GRE_faction_gui_flag }
                        
                    set_temp_variable = { tmp_mon_effect_increase = 10 }
                    set_temp_variable = { tmp_mon_effect = fct_mon_effect_multiplier }
                    add_to_temp_variable = { tmp_mon_effect = tmp_mon_effect_increase }
                    set_variable = { fct_mon_effect_multiplier = tmp_mon_effect }
                    #########  ############
                    custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_fct_effect_multiplier_change_shrt_title
                    custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_fct_effect_multiplier_change_shrt_up_mon
                    ########
                    set_temp_dem_adverse = yes
                    set_temp_com_adverse = yes
                    set_temp_fas_beneficial = yes
                    set_temp_mon_favourable = yes
                }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = { check_variable = { decision_taken = 1 } }
                custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_drakos_selection_tt
                ###[ FACTION MECHANICS ]###
                if={
                    limit={ has_country_flag=GRE_faction_gui_flag }
                        
                    set_temp_variable = { tmp_mon_effect_increase = 6 }
                    set_temp_variable = { tmp_mon_effect = fct_mon_effect_multiplier }
                    add_to_temp_variable = { tmp_mon_effect = tmp_mon_effect_increase }
                    set_variable = { fct_mon_effect_multiplier = tmp_mon_effect }
                    set_temp_variable = { tmp_dem_effect_increase = 4 }
                    set_temp_variable = { tmp_dem_effect = fct_dem_effect_multiplier }
                    add_to_temp_variable = { tmp_dem_effect = tmp_dem_effect_increase }

unit_leader_event = {               # Convicted to Death Generals
	id = hellas.14
	title = hellas.14.t
	desc = hellas.14.desc

    timeout_days = 14

        name = hellas.14.a
        ai_chance = { base = 100 }
        hidden_effect = {
            every_character = {
                limit = { has_character_flag = wanted_for_dead }
                clr_character_flag = wanted_for_dead
            }
        }
        custom_effect_tooltip = h14_a
        #######################
        set_temp_variable = { tmp_dem_effect_increase = 1.5 }
        set_temp_variable = { tmp_dem_effect = fct_dem_effect_multiplier }
        add_to_temp_variable = { tmp_dem_effect = tmp_dem_effect_increase }
        set_variable = { fct_dem_effect_multiplier = tmp_dem_effect }
        set_temp_variable = { tmp_com_effect_increase = 0.5 }
        set_temp_variable = { tmp_com_effect = fct_com_effect_multiplier }
        add_to_temp_variable = { tmp_com_effect = tmp_com_effect_increase }
        set_variable = { fct_com_effect_multiplier = tmp_com_effect }

        ###[ FACTION MECHANICS ]###
            if={
                limit={ has_country_flag=GRE_faction_gui_flag }
				
            set_temp_dem_beneficial = yes
            set_temp_com_slightly_beneficial = yes
        }
        ######[REPORT EVENTS]######

        set_temp_variable = { tmpREAC2=63 }

        set_temp_variable = { CD=1 }

country_event = {
	id = hellas.17
	title = hellas.17.t
	desc = hellas.17.desc
    picture = GFX_report_event_monarchists_power_up

	trigger={
        tag=GRE
        check_variable={ fct_mon_effect_multiplier<400 }
        has_country_flag=GRE_kathestos_proclaimed
        has_country_flag=GRE_faction_gui_flag
        is_any_faction_rebellious=no
    }

    mean_time_to_happen={
        days=30
        modifier={
            if={
                limit={ check_variable={ var=GRE.final_mon_military_weight value=5 compare=less_than_or_equals }}

                set_temp_variable={ amnt=1000 }
            }
            else={
                set_temp_variable={ x=GRE.final_mon_military_weight }
                set_temp_variable={ tmpLWTHR=5 }
                set_temp_variable={ tmpUPTHR=60 }
                set_temp_variable = { tmpMAXDIR=0 }
                in_trigger_calculate_upper_lower_bounded_y_ax_b=yes
                multiply_temp_variable={ y=100 }
                set_temp_variable={ amnt=y }
            }
            add=amnt
        }
	}

	fire_only_once=no
    timeout_days=3
	
	option = {
		name = hellas.17.a
        #
        if={
            limit={ is_any_faction_rebellious=yes }
            set_temp_variable_to_random={ var=tmp_mon_effect_increase min=4 max=6}
            multiply_temp_variable={ tmp_mon_effect=fct_mon_effect_multiplier }
            set_temp_variable={ tmp_mon_effect=fct_mon_effect_multiplier }
            add_to_temp_variable={ tmp_mon_effect=tmp_mon_effect_increase }
            set_variable={ fct_mon_effect_multiplier=tmp_mon_effect }
            #########
            custom_effect_tooltip=GRE_fct_effect_multiplier_change_shrt_title
            custom_effect_tooltip=GRE_fct_effect_multiplier_change_shrt_up_mon
            custom_effect_tooltip=GRE_fct_effect_multiplier_over_200_danger_tt
        }
        else={ 
            set_temp_variable_to_random={ var=tmp_mon_effect_increase min=4 max=6 }
            set_temp_variable={ tmp_mon_effect=fct_mon_effect_multiplier }
            add_to_temp_variable={ tmp_mon_effect=tmp_mon_effect_increase }
            set_variable={ fct_mon_effect_multiplier=tmp_mon_effect }
            set_temp_variable={ decrease_val=tmp_mon_effect_increase }
            divide_temp_variable={ decrease_val=3 }
            set_temp_variable={ tmp_dem_effect_decrease=decrease_val }
            set_temp_variable={ tmp_dem_effect=fct_dem_effect_multiplier }
            subtract_from_temp_variable={ tmp_dem_effect=tmp_dem_effect_decrease }
            set_variable={ fct_dem_effect_multiplier=tmp_dem_effect }
            set_temp_variable={ tmp_com_effect_decrease=decrease_val }
            set_temp_variable={ tmp_com_effect=fct_com_effect_multiplier }
            subtract_from_temp_variable={ tmp_com_effect=tmp_com_effect_decrease }
            set_variable={ fct_com_effect_multiplier=tmp_com_effect }
            set_temp_variable={ tmp_fas_effect_decrease=decrease_val }
            set_temp_variable={ tmp_fas_effect=fct_fas_effect_multiplier }
            subtract_from_temp_variable={ tmp_fas_effect=tmp_fas_effect_decrease }
            set_variable={ fct_fas_effect_multiplier=tmp_fas_effect }
            #########
            custom_effect_tooltip=GRE_fct_effect_multiplier_change_shrt_title
            custom_effect_tooltip=GRE_fct_effect_multiplier_change_shrt_down_dem
            custom_effect_tooltip=GRE_fct_effect_multiplier_change_shrt_down_com
            custom_effect_tooltip=GRE_fct_effect_multiplier_change_shrt_down_fas
            custom_effect_tooltip=GRE_fct_effect_multiplier_change_shrt_up_mon
        }
        GRE_faction_mon_refresh=yes
    }
}

        has_country_flag=GRE_faction_gui_flag
        is_any_faction_rebellious=no
        check_variable={ var=fct_fas value=95 compare=less_than }
    }

    mean_time_to_happen = {
        days=10
        modifier={
            if={
                limit={ check_variable={ var=GRE.final_fas_military_weight value=5 compare=less_than_or_equals }}

                set_temp_variable={ amnt=1000 }
            }
            else={
                set_temp_variable={ x=GRE.final_fas_military_weight }
                set_temp_variable={ tmpLWTHR=5 }
                set_temp_variable={ tmpUPTHR=100 }
                set_temp_variable = { tmpMAXDIR=0 }
                in_trigger_calculate_upper_lower_bounded_y_ax_b=yes
                multiply_temp_variable={ y=100 }
                set_temp_variable={ amnt=y }
            }
            add=amnt
        }
	}

	fire_only_once=no
    timeout_days=3
	
	option = {
		name = hellas.20.a
        #
        if={
            limit={ is_any_faction_rebellious=yes }
            set_temp_variable_to_random={ var=tmp_fas_effect_increase min=4 max=6}
            multiply_temp_variable={ tmp_fas_effect=fct_fas_effect_multiplier }
            set_temp_variable={ tmp_fas_effect=fct_fas_effect_multiplier }
            add_to_temp_variable={ tmp_fas_effect=tmp_fas_effect_increase }
            set_variable={ fct_fas_effect_multiplier=tmp_fas_effect }
            #########
            custom_effect_tooltip=GRE_fct_effect_multiplier_change_shrt_title
            custom_effect_tooltip=GRE_fct_effect_multiplier_change_shrt_up_fas
            custom_effect_tooltip=GRE_fct_effect_multiplier_over_200_danger_tt
        }
        else={
            set_temp_variable_to_random={ var=tmp_fas_effect_increase min=4 max=6 }
            set_temp_variable={ tmp_fas_effect=fct_fas_effect_multiplier }
            add_to_temp_variable={ tmp_fas_effect=tmp_fas_effect_increase }
            set_variable={ fct_fas_effect_multiplier=tmp_fas_effect }
            set_temp_variable={ decrease_val=tmp_fas_effect_increase }
            divide_temp_variable={ decrease_val=3 }
            set_temp_variable={ tmp_dem_effect_decrease=decrease_val }
            set_temp_variable={ tmp_dem_effect=fct_dem_effect_multiplier }
            subtract_from_temp_variable={ tmp_dem_effect=tmp_dem_effect_decrease }
            set_variable={ fct_dem_effect_multiplier=tmp_dem_effect }
            set_temp_variable={ tmp_mon_effect_decrease=decrease_val }
            set_temp_variable={ tmp_mon_effect=fct_mon_effect_multiplier }
            subtract_from_temp_variable={ tmp_mon_effect=tmp_mon_effect_decrease }
            set_variable={ fct_mon_effect_multiplier=tmp_mon_effect }
            set_temp_variable={ tmp_com_effect_decrease=decrease_val }
            set_temp_variable={ tmp_com_effect=fct_com_effect_multiplier }
            subtract_from_temp_variable={ tmp_com_effect=tmp_com_effect_decrease }
            set_variable={ fct_com_effect_multiplier=tmp_com_effect }
            #########
            custom_effect_tooltip=GRE_fct_effect_multiplier_change_shrt_title
            custom_effect_tooltip=GRE_fct_effect_multiplier_change_shrt_down_dem
            custom_effect_tooltip=GRE_fct_effect_multiplier_change_shrt_down_com
            custom_effect_tooltip=GRE_fct_effect_multiplier_change_shrt_up_fas
            custom_effect_tooltip=GRE_fct_effect_multiplier_change_shrt_down_mon
        }
        GRE_faction_mon_refresh=yes
    }
}

state_event = {                                                                                   ## Refresh Invigorating/Working
	id = hellas.33
	title = hellas.1012.t
	desc = hellas.1012.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_greek_hs_hungry_kids

    timeout_days=1
    is_triggered_only=yes
	fire_only_once = no
    hidden = yes
    
    immediate = {
        # Here we essentially calculate all factors to reduce base days per iteration in the two missions. For avoiding conflcits, we send this state event
        # to Athens for invigorating and to Thessaloniki for working. Why we do this here and not right after re-activating the decision? Because it will not
        # work that way. Essentially you can't both activate a mission and then reduce the amount of days and since you cannot dynamically set mis_days_timeout,
        # you have a problem. Thus we send an 'event' after 4 hours, during which time the game has activated the mission and now properly understands us telling
        # it to reduce amount of days by that amount.

        hidden_effect = {
            GRE = {
                set_temp_variable = { x=stability }
                multiply_temp_variable = { x=100 }
                set_temp_variable = { tmp=amount_of_projects }
                multiply_temp_variable = { tmp=5 }
                add_to_temp_variable = { x=tmp }
                set_temp_variable = { tmp=amount_of_propaganda }
                multiply_temp_variable = { tmp=10 }
                add_to_temp_variable = { x=tmp }
                multiply_temp_variable = { x=-1 }
                if = {
                    limit = { PREV = { state=47 }}
                    add_days_mission_timeout={mission=invigorating_hellenic_spirit days=x}
                }
                else = {
                    add_days_mission_timeout={mission=workers_entering_factories days=x}
                }
            }
        }
    }

    option = {
		name = hellas.1012.a
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
    }
}

country_event = {
	id = hellas.51
	title = hellas.51.t
	desc = hellas.51.desc
    picture = GFX_report_event_monarchists_power_up

	trigger={
        tag=GRE
        check_variable={ var=fct_mon value=95 compare=greater_than_or_equals }
        has_country_flag=GRE_faction_gui_flag
    }

	fire_only_once=yes

    immediate={
        # Max benefits are granted if debt is cleared up to: 1.1.1937
        # Subsequently a % of benefits is lost per day.

        set_temp_variable={ cday=GRE.MON_LOYALTY_ACHIEVED_DAYS }
        subtract_from_temp_variable={ cday=707006 } # 1rst of January 1937
        set_variable={ h51_days_delayed_raw=cday }
        set_temp_variable={ x=cday }
        set_temp_variable={ tmpLWTHR=0 }
        set_temp_variable={ tmpUPTHR=550 }
        set_temp_variable={ tmpMAXDIR=0 }
        calculate_upper_lower_bounded_y_ax_b=yes
        multiply_temp_variable={ y=0.9 }
        add_to_temp_variable={ y=0.1 }                          # y = 0.9x + 0.1 (therefore minimum 10% of benefits)
        set_variable={ h51_multiplier=y }
    }
	
	option = {
		name = hellas.51.a

        multiply_temp_variable={ stab_bonus?0.025=h51_multiplier }
        multiply_temp_variable={ wsup_bonus?0.025=h51_multiplier }
        multiply_temp_variable={ stat_bonus?0.05=h51_multiplier }
        multiply_temp_variable={ rinf_bonus?5.00=h51_multiplier }
        multiply_temp_variable={ iinf_bonus?2.50=h51_multiplier }
        add_stability=stab_bonus
        add_war_support=wsup_bonus
        ###[ BOP MECHANIC ]###
        set_temp_variable={ tmpMOV=stat_bonus }
        fluctuate_bop_by_tmpMOV_tmpTT=yes
        every_country={
            limit={
                is_in_array={
                    array=GRE.important_nations
                    value=THIS.id
                }
                has_government=neutrality
            }
            set_temp_variable={ findX=THIS.id }
            set_temp_variable={ findY=rinf_bonus }
            set_temp_variable={ favTT=2 }
            fluctuate_favor_with_findX_by_findY=yes
        }
        every_country={
            limit={
                is_in_array={
                    array=GRE.important_nations
                    value=THIS.id
                }
                NOT={ has_government=neutrality }
            }
            set_temp_variable={ findX=THIS.id }
            set_temp_variable={ findY=iinf_bonus }
            set_temp_variable={ favTT=2 }
            fluctuate_favor_with_findX_by_findY=yes
        }
        custom_effect_tooltip=h51_bonuses_expl_tt
        #
        add_to_variable={ loyalties_secured=1 }
        clear_variable=h51_multiplier
    }
}

        multiply_temp_variable={ y=0.9 }
        add_to_temp_variable={ y=0.1 }                          # y = 0.9x + 0.1 (therefore minimum 10% of benefits)
        set_variable={ h54_multiplier=y }
    }
	
	option = {
		name = hellas.54.a

        multiply_temp_variable={ stab_bonus?0.025=h54_multiplier }
        multiply_temp_variable={ wsup_bonus?0.025=h54_multiplier }
        multiply_temp_variable={ stat_bonus?0.05=h54_multiplier }
        multiply_temp_variable={ rinf_bonus?5.00=h54_multiplier }
        multiply_temp_variable={ iinf_bonus?2.50=h54_multiplier }
        add_stability=stab_bonus
        add_war_support=wsup_bonus
        ###[ BOP MECHANIC ]###
        set_temp_variable={ tmpMOV=stat_bonus }
        fluctuate_bop_by_tmpMOV_tmpTT=yes
        every_country={
            limit={
                is_in_array={
                    array=GRE.important_nations
                    value=THIS.id
                }
                has_government=fascism
            }
            set_temp_variable={ findX=THIS.id }
            set_temp_variable={ findY=rinf_bonus }
            set_temp_variable={ favTT=2 }
            fluctuate_favor_with_findX_by_findY=yes
        }
        every_country={
            limit={
                is_in_array={
                    array=GRE.important_nations
                    value=THIS.id
                }
                NOT={ has_government=fascism }
            }
            set_temp_variable={ findX=THIS.id }
            set_temp_variable={ findY=iinf_bonus }
            set_temp_variable={ favTT=2 }
            fluctuate_favor_with_findX_by_findY=yes
        }
        custom_effect_tooltip=h54_bonuses_expl_tt
        #
        add_to_variable={ loyalties_secured=1 }
        clear_variable=h54_multiplier
    }
}

country_event = {
	id = hellas.55
	title = hellas.55.t
	desc = hellas.55.desc
    picture = GFX_report_event_fascists_power_up

	trigger={
        tag=GRE
        check_variable={ loyalties_secured=4 }
        has_country_flag=GRE_faction_gui_flag
    }

	fire_only_once=yes

    immediate={
        # Max benefits are granted if debt is cleared up to: 1.1.1937
        # Subsequently a % of benefits is lost per day.

        set_temp_variable={ cday=GRE.ALL_LOYALTY_ACHIEVED_DAYS }
        subtract_from_temp_variable={ cday=707187 } # 1st of July 1937
        set_variable={ h55_days_delayed_raw=cday }
        set_temp_variable={ x=cday }
        set_temp_variable={ tmpLWTHR=0 }
        set_temp_variable={ tmpUPTHR=550 }
        set_temp_variable={ tmpMAXDIR=0 }
        calculate_upper_lower_bounded_y_ax_b=yes
        multiply_temp_variable={ y=0.9 }
        add_to_temp_variable={ y=0.1 }                          # y = 0.9x + 0.1 (therefore minimum 10% of benefits)
        set_variable={ h55_multiplier=y }
    }
	
	option = {
		name = hellas.55.a

        multiply_temp_variable={ stab_bonus?0.05=h54_multiplier }
        multiply_temp_variable={ wsup_bonus?0.05=h54_multiplier }
        multiply_temp_variable={ stat_bonus?0.10=h54_multiplier }
        multiply_temp_variable={ rinf_bonus?8.00=h54_multiplier }
        add_stability=stab_bonus
        add_war_support=wsup_bonus
        ###[ BOP MECHANIC ]###
        set_temp_variable={ tmpMOV=stat_bonus }
        fluctuate_bop_by_tmpMOV_tmpTT=yes
        every_country={
            limit={
                is_in_array={
                    array=GRE.important_nations
                    value=THIS.id
                }
            }
            set_temp_variable={ findX=THIS.id }
            set_temp_variable={ findY=rinf_bonus }
            set_temp_variable={ favTT=2 }
            fluctuate_favor_with_findX_by_findY=yes
        }
        custom_effect_tooltip=h55_bonuses_expl_tt
        #
        clear_variable=loyalties_secured
    }
}

country_event = {                                                                       #Army Equipment Increases, Officer Preparation/Training increases too
	id = hellas.203
	title = hellas.203.t
	desc = hellas.203.desc
    picture = GFX_report_event_generic_weapon_cache

	trigger = {
        original_tag = GRE 
        check_variable = { preparedness_level < 1 }
        set_temp_variable = { x = num_equipment@infantry_equipment }
        add_to_temp_variable = { x = num_equipment_in_armies@infantry_equipment }
        check_variable = { x > eq_thr?10000 }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 0
	}
    
	fire_only_once = no
	
    immediate = {
        hidden_effect = {
            add_to_variable = { evnt_cnt_203 = 1 }
            add_to_variable = { eq_thr?10000 = 5000 }
        }
    }
    
	option = {
		name = hellas.203.a
        if = {
            limit = { check_variable = { evnt_cnt_203 = 1 } }
            custom_effect_tooltip = train_25_percent_of_lvl3_generals_tt
        }
        else = {
            custom_effect_tooltip = train_percent_in_order_generals_tt
        }
        hidden_effect = { activate_decision = hidden_proc_for_equip_event }
    }      
}

country_event = {                                                                        # Debt fully repaid
	id = hellas.240
	title = hellas.240.t
	desc = hellas.240.desc
    picture = GFX_report_event_bank_of_greece

	trigger = {
        original_tag = GRE
        has_country_flag = GRE_debt_free
        check_variable = { GRE.defaulted_on@ENG = 0 }
        check_variable = { GRE.defaulted_on@FRA = 0 }
        check_variable = { GRE.defaulted_on@ITA = 0 }
    }

	fire_only_once = yes

    immediate={
        # Max benefits are granted if debt is cleared up to: 1.1.1938
        # Subsequently a % of benefits is lost per day.
        set_temp_variable={ h240_cday=GRE.h240_debt_fulfilment_at_day_days }
        subtract_from_temp_variable={ h240_cday=707371 } # 1rst of January 1938
        set_variable={ h240_days_delayed_raw=h240_cday }
        set_temp_variable={ x=h240_cday }
        set_temp_variable={ tmpLWTHR=0 }
        set_temp_variable={ tmpUPTHR=550 }
        set_temp_variable={ tmpMAXDIR=0 }
        calculate_upper_lower_bounded_y_ax_b=yes
        multiply_temp_variable={ y=0.9 }
        add_to_temp_variable={ y=0.1 }                          # y = 0.9x + 0.1 (therefore minimum 10% of benefits)
        set_variable={ h240_debt_fulfilment_multiplier=y }
    }
	
	option = {
		name = hellas.240.a

        multiply_temp_variable={ stab_bonus?0.25=h240_debt_fulfilment_multiplier }
        multiply_temp_variable={ stat_bonus?0.20=h240_debt_fulfilment_multiplier }
        add_stability = stab_bonus
        ###[ BOP MECHANIC ]###
        set_temp_variable={ tmpMOV=stat_bonus }
        fluctuate_bop_by_tmpMOV_tmpTT=yes
        every_country={
            limit={ is_in_array={ array=GRE.important_nations value=THIS.id }}

            set_temp_variable={ findX=THIS.id }
            set_temp_variable={ findY=8 }
            set_temp_variable={ favTT=2 }
            fluctuate_favor_with_findX_by_findY=yes
        }        
        custom_effect_tooltip=h240_bonuses_expl_tt
    }
}

country_event = {               #MINING RIGHTS - RETURN EVENT
	id = hellas.242
	title = hellas.242.t
	desc = hellas.242.desc
    picture = GFX_report_event_land_on_sale
    is_triggered_only = yes
    fire_only_once = no

    immediate = {
        hidden_effect = {

            set_temp_variable={ tmpID=241 }
            event_info_gui_add_current_event_to_heap=yes
            set_variable={ iterations = h241_id^num }
            while_loop_effect={
                break=br
                limit={ always=yes }
                
                if={ limit={ check_variable={ h241_id^num=0 }} set_temp_variable={ br=1 }}
                else={
                    find_highest_in_array={ array=h241_weight value=val_highest index=idx_highest }
                    add_to_array={ h241_sorted_weight=val_highest }
                    add_to_array={ h241_sorted_id=h241_id^idx_highest }
                    remove_from_array={ array=h241_weight index=idx_highest }
                    remove_from_array={ array=h241_id index=idx_highest }
                }
            }
        }
    }

    option={
        name=hellas.242.a
        trigger={ check_variable={ h241_sorted_weight^0 > 0 } }
        set_variable={ h241_return_id=h241_sorted_id^0 }
        set_variable={ h241_return_weight=h241_sorted_weight^0 }
        country_event={ id=hellas.243 days=0 }
        clear_array=h241_sorted_id
        clear_array=h241_sorted_weight
        clear_array=h241_weight
        clear_array=h241_id

country_event = {               #BRITISH RESPONSE
	id = hellas.3095
    title = { text = hellas.3095.t_a trigger = { check_variable = { opt = 1 } } }
    title = { text = hellas.3095.t_b trigger = { check_variable = { opt = 2 } } }
    title = { text = hellas.3095.t_c trigger = { check_variable = { opt = 3 } } }
    title = { text = hellas.3095.t_d trigger = { check_variable = { opt = 4 } } }
	desc = { text = hellas.3095.desc_a trigger = { check_variable = { opt = 1 } } }
    desc = { text = hellas.3095.desc_b trigger = { check_variable = { opt = 2 } } }
    desc = { text = hellas.3095.desc_c trigger = { check_variable = { opt = 3 } } }
    desc = { text = hellas.3095.desc_d trigger = { check_variable = { opt = 4 } } }
    picture = GFX_report_event_belgrade_1939

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

    immediate = {
        hidden_effect = {
            ###[British Influence]###
            if = {
                limit = {
                    check_variable = { var=ENG.favor@GRE value=-60 compare=less_than }
                }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b1 = 0 }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b2 = 0 }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b3 = 10 }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b4 = 90 }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    check_variable = { var=ENG.favor@GRE value=-60 compare=greater_than_or_equals }
                    check_variable = { var=ENG.favor@GRE value=-30 compare=less_than }
                }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b1 = 0 }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b2 = 5 }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b3 = 15 }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b4 = 80 }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    check_variable = { var=ENG.favor@GRE value=-30 compare=greater_than_or_equals }
                    check_variable = { var=ENG.favor@GRE value=0 compare=less_than }
                }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b1 = 5 }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b2 = 10 }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b3 = 15 }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b4 = 70 }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    check_variable = { var=ENG.favor@GRE value=0 compare=greater_than_or_equals }
                    check_variable = { var=ENG.favor@GRE value=30 compare=less_than }
                }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b1 = 10 }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b2 = 20 }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b3 = 30 }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b4 = 40 }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    check_variable = { var=ENG.favor@GRE value=30 compare=greater_than_or_equals }
                    check_variable = { var=ENG.favor@GRE value=40 compare=less_than }
                }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b1 = 20 }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b2 = 30 }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b3 = 30 }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b4 = 20 }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    check_variable = { var=ENG.favor@GRE value=40 compare=greater_than_or_equals }
                    check_variable = { var=ENG.favor@GRE value=50 compare=less_than }
                }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b1 = 25 }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b2 = 50 }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b3 = 15 }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b4 = 10 }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    check_variable = { var=ENG.favor@GRE value=50 compare=greater_than_or_equals }
                    check_variable = { var=ENG.favor@GRE value=60 compare=less_than }
                }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b1 = 35 }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b2 = 50 }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b3 = 10 }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b4 = 5 }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    check_variable = { var=ENG.favor@GRE value=70 compare=greater_than_or_equals }
                    check_variable = { var=ENG.favor@GRE value=80 compare=less_than }
                }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b1 = 50 }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b2 = 40 }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b3 = 10 }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b4 = 0 }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    check_variable = { var=ENG.favor@GRE value=80 compare=greater_than_or_equals }
                    check_variable = { var=ENG.favor@GRE value=90 compare=less_than }
                }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b1 = 60 }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b2 = 30 }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b3 = 10 }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b4 = 0 }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    check_variable = { var=ENG.favor@GRE value=90 compare=greater_than_or_equals }
                    check_variable = { var=ENG.favor@GRE value=95 compare=less_than }
                }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b1 = 80 }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b2 = 20 }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b3 = 0 }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b4 = 0 }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    check_variable = { var=ENG.favor@GRE value=95 compare=greater_than_or_equals }
                    check_variable = { var=ENG.favor@GRE value=100 compare=less_than_or_equals }
                }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b1 = 100 }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b2 = 0 }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b3 = 0 }
                add_to_temp_variable = { b4 = 0 }
            }
            ###[AXAL]###
            if = { limit = { check_variable = { GRE.alax < 5 } } add_to_temp_variable = { b1 = 0 } add_to_temp_variable = { b2 = 0 } add_to_temp_variable = { b3 = 0 } add_to_temp_variable = { b4 = 100 } }
            else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { GRE.alax < 10 } } add_to_temp_variable = { b1 = 0 } add_to_temp_variable = { b2 = 0 } add_to_temp_variable = { b3 = 25 } add_to_temp_variable = { b4 = 75 } }
            else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { GRE.alax < 20 } } add_to_temp_variable = { b1 = 0 } add_to_temp_variable = { b2 = 10 } add_to_temp_variable = { b3 = 20 } add_to_temp_variable = { b4 = 70 } }
            else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { GRE.alax < 30 } } add_to_temp_variable = { b1 = 10 } add_to_temp_variable = { b2 = 20 } add_to_temp_variable = { b3 = 30 } add_to_temp_variable = { b4 = 40 } }
            else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { GRE.alax < 40.01 } } add_to_temp_variable = { b1 = 10 } add_to_temp_variable = { b2 = 30 } add_to_temp_variable = { b3 = 30 } add_to_temp_variable = { b4 = 30 } }
            else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { GRE.alax < 59.99 } } add_to_temp_variable = { b1 = 25 } add_to_temp_variable = { b2 = 25 } add_to_temp_variable = { b3 = 25 } add_to_temp_variable = { b4 = 25 } }
            else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { GRE.alax < 70 } } add_to_temp_variable = { b1 = 30 } add_to_temp_variable = { b2 = 30 } add_to_temp_variable = { b3 = 30 } add_to_temp_variable = { b4 = 10 } }
            else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { GRE.alax < 80 } } add_to_temp_variable = { b1 = 40 } add_to_temp_variable = { b2 = 30 } add_to_temp_variable = { b3 = 20 } add_to_temp_variable = { b4 = 10 } }
            else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { GRE.alax < 90 } } add_to_temp_variable = { b1 = 70 } add_to_temp_variable = { b2 = 20 } add_to_temp_variable = { b3 = 10 } add_to_temp_variable = { b4 = 0 } }
            else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { GRE.alax < 95.01 } } add_to_temp_variable = { b1 = 75 } add_to_temp_variable = { b2 = 25 } add_to_temp_variable = { b3 = 0 } add_to_temp_variable = { b4 = 0 } }
            else = { add_to_temp_variable = { b1 = 100 } add_to_temp_variable = { b2 = 0 } add_to_temp_variable = { b3 = 0 } add_to_temp_variable = { b4 = 0 } }
            ###[BASE BIAS]###
            add_to_temp_variable = { b1 = 30 } 
            add_to_temp_variable = { b2 = 30 } 
            add_to_temp_variable = { b3 = 30 } 
            add_to_temp_variable = { b4 = 10 }
            ###[AVERAGE]###
            divide_temp_variable = { b1 = 3 }
            divide_temp_variable = { b2 = 3 }
            divide_temp_variable = { b3 = 3 }
            divide_temp_variable = { b4 = 3 }
            ###[PROTEST LEVEL ADJUSTMENTS]###
            if = { 
                limit = { check_variable = { GRE.protest_level = 4 } }
                multiply_temp_variable = { b1 = 2.00 }   #100%higher
                multiply_temp_variable = { b2 = 1.50 }   #50%higher
                multiply_temp_variable = { b3 = 0.50 }   #50%lower
                multiply_temp_variable = { b4 = 0.10 }   #90%lower
            }
            else_if = { 
                limit = { check_variable = { GRE.protest_level = 3 } }
                multiply_temp_variable = { b1 = 1.75 }   #75%higher
                multiply_temp_variable = { b2 = 1.25 }   #25%higher
                multiply_temp_variable = { b3 = 0.75 }   #25%lower
                multiply_temp_variable = { b4 = 0.25 }   #75%lower
            }
            else_if = { 
                limit = { check_variable = { GRE.protest_level = 2 } }
                multiply_temp_variable = { b1 = 1.50 }   #50%higher
                multiply_temp_variable = { b2 = 1.25 }   #25%higher
                multiply_temp_variable = { b3 = 0.75 }   #25%lower
                multiply_temp_variable = { b4 = 0.50 }   #50%lower
            }
            #log="[?b1]"
            #log="[?b2]"
            #log="[?b3]"
            #log="[?b4]"
            ###[FINAL]###
            random_list = {
                seed = random
                var:b1 = { set_variable = { opt = 1 } }
                var:b2 = { set_variable = { opt = 2 } }
                var:b3 = { set_variable = { opt = 3 } }
                var:b4 = { set_variable = { opt = 4 } }
            }
        }
    }
	
	option = { # Best Result
		name = hellas.3095.a
        trigger = { check_variable = { opt = 1 } }
        add_political_power = 150
        add_stability = 0.1
        add_war_support = 0.1
        every_country = {
            limit = { has_country_flag=balkan_pact_reinforced NOT={has_country_flag=GRE_kathestos_proclaimed} }
            add_political_power = 75
            add_stability = 0.05
            add_war_support = 0.05
            set_temp_variable={ tmpAW=8 } 
            add_to_variable = { balkan_pact_desirability=tmpAW } 
            custom_effect_tooltip = alliance_weight_increased_tmpAW_tt
        }
        set_temp_variable = { findX = ENG.id }
        set_temp_variable = { findY = 5 }
        fluctuate_favor_with_findX_by_findY=yes
        clear_variable = opt
        clear_variable = protest_level
    }
    option = { # 2nd Best Result
		name = hellas.3095.b
        trigger = { check_variable = { opt = 2 } }
        add_political_power = 75
        add_stability = 0.05
        add_war_support = 0.05
        every_country = {
            limit = { has_country_flag = balkan_pact_reinforced NOT={has_country_flag=GRE_kathestos_proclaimed} }
            add_political_power = 25
            add_stability = 0.02
            add_war_support = 0.02
            set_temp_variable={ tmpAW=4 } 
            add_to_variable = { balkan_pact_desirability=tmpAW } 
            custom_effect_tooltip = alliance_weight_increased_tmpAW_tt
        }
        set_temp_variable = { findX = ENG.id }
        set_temp_variable = { findY = 5 }
        fluctuate_favor_with_findX_by_findY=yes
        clear_variable = opt
        clear_variable = protest_level
    }  
    option = { # 2nd Worst Result
		name = hellas.3095.c
        trigger = { check_variable = { opt = 3 } }
        add_political_power = -75
        add_stability = -0.05
        add_war_support = -0.05
        every_country = {
            limit = { has_country_flag = balkan_pact_reinforced NOT={has_country_flag=GRE_kathestos_proclaimed} }
            add_political_power = -25
            add_stability = -0.02
            add_war_support = -0.02
            set_temp_variable={ tmpAW=-4 } 
            add_to_variable = { balkan_pact_desirability=tmpAW } 
            custom_effect_tooltip = alliance_weight_decreased_tmpAW_tt
        }
        set_temp_variable = { findX = ENG.id }
        set_temp_variable = { findY = -5 }
        fluctuate_favor_with_findX_by_findY=yes
        clear_variable = opt
        clear_variable = protest_level
    }
    option = { # Worst Result
		name = hellas.3095.d
        trigger = { check_variable = { opt = 4 } }
        add_political_power = -150
        add_stability = -0.1
        add_war_support = -0.1
        every_country = {
            limit = { has_country_flag = balkan_pact_reinforced NOT={has_country_flag=GRE_kathestos_proclaimed} }
            add_political_power = -75
            add_stability = -0.05
            add_war_support = -0.05
            set_temp_variable={ tmpAW=-8 } 
            add_to_variable = { balkan_pact_desirability=tmpAW } 
            custom_effect_tooltip = alliance_weight_decreased_tmpAW_tt
        }
        set_temp_variable = { findX = ENG.id }
        set_temp_variable = { findY = -5 }
        fluctuate_favor_with_findX_by_findY=yes
        clear_variable = opt
        clear_variable = protest_level
    }

country_event = {               #THE PRO-AXIS PLOT
	id = hellas.317
	title = hellas.317.t
	desc = {                                                                                        ## Greece was denied by the Germans
        text = hellas.317.desc
        trigger = {
            has_country_flag = prepared_for_1940_plot
            has_country_flag = GRE_kotzias_safe_removal
        }
    }
    picture = GFX_report_event_1940_plot

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes
    
    immediate = {
        hidden_effect = {
            set_country_flag = GRE_plot_occurred
        }
    }
	
	option = {                                      ## Went in prepared
		name = hellas.317.a
        trigger = {
            has_country_flag = prepared_for_1940_plot
            GRE_kostas_kotzias = { has_character_flag = GRE_kotzias_safe_removal }
        }
        add_political_power = 400
        set_temp_variable = { tmp_mon_effect_increase = 25 }
        set_temp_variable = { tmp_mon_effect = fct_mon_effect_multiplier }
        add_to_temp_variable = { tmp_mon_effect = tmp_mon_effect_increase }
        set_variable = { fct_mon_effect_multiplier = tmp_mon_effect }
        #########  ############
        custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_fct_effect_multiplier_change_shrt_title
        custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_fct_effect_multiplier_change_shrt_up_mon
    }  

    option = {                                      ## Went in partially unprepared
		name = hellas.317.b
        trigger = {
            OR = {
                AND = {
                    has_country_flag = prepared_for_1940_plot
                    NOT = { GRE_kostas_kotzias = { has_character_flag = GRE_kotzias_safe_removal } }
                }
                AND = {
                    has_country_flag = GRE_kotzias_safe_removal
                    NOT = { GRE_kostas_kotzias = { has_character_flag = GRE_kotzias_safe_removal } }
                }
            }
        }
        add_political_power = -100
        add_stability = -0.1
        add_war_support = -0.05
    } 
    
    option = {                                      ## Went in completely unprepared
		name = hellas.317.c
        trigger = {
            NOT = { has_country_flag = prepared_for_1940_plot }
            NOT = { GRE_kostas_kotzias = { has_character_flag = GRE_kotzias_safe_removal } }
        }
        add_political_power = -400
        add_stability = -0.4
        add_war_support = -0.2
        set_temp_variable = { tmp_mon_effect_increase = -25 }
        set_temp_variable = { tmp_mon_effect = fct_mon_effect_multiplier }
        subtract_from_temp_variable = { tmp_mon_effect = tmp_mon_effect_increase }

        custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_fct_effect_multiplier_change_shrt_up_mon
    }
}

    }

country_event = {                               # BRITISH DEAL
	id = hellas.3182
	title = hellas.3182.t
	desc = hellas.3182.desc
    picture = GFX_report_event_trade

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {  ### BRITAIN ACCEPTS
		name = hellas.3182.a    
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 1000
				check_variable = { var = ENG.favor@GRE value = 80 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
			}
		}
        GRE = { add_political_power = 300 }
        add_political_power = 75
        ENG = {
            diplomatic_relation = {
                country = GRE
                relation = guarantee
                active = yes
            }        
        }
        ENG = {
            diplomatic_relation = {
                country = GRE
                relation = non_aggression_pact
                active = yes
            }        
        }
        GRE = {
            diplomatic_relation = {
                country = ENG
                relation = non_aggression_pact
                active = yes
            } 
        }
        ENG = {
            diplomatic_relation = {
                country = GRE
                relation = docking_rights
                active = yes
            }        
        }
        GRE = {
            diplomatic_relation = {
                country = ENG
                relation = docking_rights
                active = yes
            }  
        }
        ### THE FOLLOWING BLOCK ADDS A MASSIVE BOOST OF FAVOR TO UK AND THEIR ALLIES. LIKEWISE SUBTRACTS A MASSIVE AMOUNT OF FAVOR FROM THEIR ENEMIES.
        hidden_effect = {
            every_country = {
                limit = {
                    is_in_array = {
                        array = global.favor_mechanic
                        value = THIS.id
                    }
                }
                if = {
                    limit = {
                        OR = {
                            is_in_faction_with = ENG
                            AND = {
                                original_tag = USA
                                has_government = democratic
                                ENG = { has_government = democratic }
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    add_to_variable = { THIS.favor@GRE = 30 }
                }
                else_if = {
                    limit = {
                        OR = {
                            original_tag = GER
                            original_tag = ITA
                            original_tag = BUL
                        }
                        NOT = { is_in_faction_with = ENG }
                    }
                    if = {
                        limit = {
                            original_tag = GER
                        }
                        subtract_from_variable = { THIS.favor@GRE = 20 } 
                    }
                    else = {
                        subtract_from_variable = { THIS.favor@GRE = 30 }   
                    } 
                }
            } 
        }
        news_event = { id = hellenic_news.200 days = 0 }
    }  
	option = {  ### BRITAIN DECLINES
		name = hellas.3182.b    
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				check_variable = { var = ENG.favor@GRE value = 80 compare = less_than }
			}
		}        
        GRE = { add_political_power = 150 }  
        hidden_effect = {
            every_country = {
                limit = {
                    is_in_array = {
                        array = global.favor_mechanic
                        value = THIS.id
                    }
                }
                if = {
                    limit = {
                        OR = {
                            is_in_faction_with = ENG
                            AND = {
                                original_tag = USA
                                has_government = democratic
                                ENG = { has_government = democratic }
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    add_to_variable = { THIS.favor@GRE = 5 }
                }
            }
        }        
    }

	id = hellas.3321
	title = hellas.332.t
	desc = hellas.332.desc
    picture = "[GetEvent332Picture]"

    timeout_days=0
	is_triggered_only = yes
    immediate={
        hidden_effect={
            if = { limit={ check_variable={ THIS.id=ENG.id }} add_to_temp_array={ receivers_to_check=FRA.id } add_to_temp_array={ receivers_to_check=ITA.id }}
            else_if = { limit={ check_variable={ THIS.id=FRA.id }} add_to_temp_array={ receivers_to_check=ENG.id } add_to_temp_array={ receivers_to_check=ITA.id }}
            else_if = { limit={ check_variable={ THIS.id=ITA.id }} add_to_temp_array={ receivers_to_check=FRA.id } add_to_temp_array={ receivers_to_check=ENG.id }}
            clr_country_flag = debt_check_event_fired
            for_each_loop={
                array=receivers_to_check
                
                if={
                    limit={ check_variable={ gre_total_paid@var:v>0 }}
                
                    #log="SCOPE IS: [?THIS.GetName], checking for: [?v.GetName]"
                    clear_temp_array = tmpCHANCES
                    clear_temp_array = tmpRECEIVERS
                    clear_temp_array = tmpWEIGHT
                    set_temp_variable = { tmpSCALEMAG=1 }
                    set_temp_variable = { cred_paid=v }
                    calculate_THIS_debt_difference_chance_to_avoid_event=yes
                    calculate_final_b1_b2_from_temporary_array_tmpCHANCES_with_tmpWEIGHT_and_mode_tmpMODE=yes
                    add_to_temp_array = { tmpRECEIVERS=THIS.id }
                    set_temp_variable = { tmpREAC1=50 }
                    potentially_send_report_events_for_action_tmpREAC1_with_args_tmpARRVAL_tmpMAG_to_targets_tmpRECEIVERS=yes
                    clear_variable = gre_times_paid@THIS
                    clear_variable = gre_total_paid@THIS
                }
            }
        }
    }
	fire_only_once = no
	
	option = {
        name = hellas.332.a
    }
}

        clear_variable = FROM.e332_6_MAG@GRE
        clear_array    = FROM.e332_6_ARRVAL
    }

country_event = {                                       # REACTION TO ACTION EVENT (#7)
	id = hellas.3320007
	title = "[GetEvent332Title]"
    desc = "[GetEvent332Desc]"
    picture = "[GetEvent332Picture]"

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = no

    immediate = {
        hidden_effect = {
            ###[Set & Reset]###
            set_temp_variable = { TYPE=FROM.e332_7_t@GRE }
            ###[Effects]###

        }
    }
	
	option = {
        name=hellas.332.a
        trigger = { NOT={ check_variable={ FROM.e332_1_t@GRE=66 }}}
        if = {
            limit = {check_variable={ FROM.e332_7_t@GRE=50 }}
            set_temp_variable = { findX=FROM.id }
            set_temp_variable = { findY=-5 }
            fluctuate_favor_with_findX_by_findY=yes
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { OR={ check_variable={ FROM.e332_7_t@GRE=60 } check_variable={FROM.e332_7_t@GRE=62 }}}
            set_temp_variable = { findX=FROM.id }
            set_temp_variable_to_random = { var=findY min=0.25 max=3 integer=no }
            fluctuate_favor_with_findX_by_findY=yes
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { OR={ check_variable={ FROM.e332_7_t@GRE=61 } check_variable={FROM.e332_7_t@GRE=63 }}}
            set_temp_variable = { findX=FROM.id }
            set_temp_variable_to_random = { var=findY min=-3 max=-0.25 integer=no }
            fluctuate_favor_with_findX_by_findY=yes
        }
        ###[Clear FROM from Array]### (HAS TO BE HERE BECAUSE IN IMMEDIATE IT WON'T WORK AND CAUSE SUBSEQUENT EVENTS TO FAIL)
        remove_from_array = { GRE.e_332_7 = FROM.id }
        clear_variable = FROM.e332_7_t@GRE
        clear_variable = FROM.e332_7_MAG@GRE
        clear_array    = FROM.e332_7_ARRVAL
    }
}

country_event = {
	id = hellas.350
	title = hellas.350.t
	desc = hellas.350.desc
    picture = GFX_report_event_maniadakis_rounding_up

	trigger = {
        has_active_mission = GRE_comm_upr
        check_variable = { days_mission_timeout@GRE_comm_upr < 120 }
    }

    mean_time_to_happen = {
        days = 160
        modifier = {
            set_temp_variable = { cnt = amount_of_work_in_asfaleia }
            set_temp_variable = { final = 1 }
            set_temp_variable = { weight = 0.05 }
            multiply_temp_variable = { weight = cnt }
            subtract_from_temp_variable = { final = weight }
            factor = final
            check_variable = { days_mission_timeout@GRE_comm_upr < 181 }
        }
        modifier = {
            factor = 1.25
            check_variable = { days_mission_timeout@GRE_comm_upr > 180 }
        }
	}

	fire_only_once = no
	
	option = {
		name = hellas.350.a

        add_days_mission_timeout = {
            mission = GRE_comm_upr
            days = 30
        }
    }  
}

# Once we get into rebellious mode (active mission), we get these automatically per chance calculated.
# Once we get outside rebellious mode (mission ends), we get one more proc at random to end the series of events.

country_event = {
	id=hellas.352
	title={ text=hellas.352a.t trigger={ check_variable={ fct_dem < 40 }}}
	title={ text=hellas.352b.t trigger={ check_variable={ var=fct_dem value=40 compare=greater_than_or_equals }}}
	desc={ text=hellas.352a.desc trigger={ check_variable={ fct_dem < 40 }}}
	desc={ text=hellas.352b.desc trigger={ check_variable={ var=fct_dem value=40 compare=greater_than_or_equals }}}
    picture=GFX_report_event_republicans_rebellious

    trigger={
        has_country_flag=republicans_rebellious_initiated
        check_variable={ var=fct_dem value=40 compare=greater_than_or_equals }
    }

    mean_time_to_happen={ days=7 }
	fire_only_once=no
    timeout_days=3
	
	option={
		name=hellas.352.a
        trigger={ check_variable={ fct_dem < 40 }}

        if={
            limit={ NOT={ has_country_flag=republicans_rebellious_initiated }}
            set_country_flag=republicans_rebellious_initiated
        }
        ###[BoP]###
        set_temp_variable_to_random={ var=tmpMOV min=-0.010 max=-0.002 }
        fluctuate_bop_by_tmpMOV_tmpTT=yes
        ###[Increase Overall Effect Multiplier]###
        set_temp_variable_to_random={ var=tmp_dem_effect_increase min=6 max=14 }
        set_temp_variable={ tmp_dem_effect=fct_dem_effect_multiplier }
        add_to_temp_variable={ tmp_dem_effect=tmp_dem_effect_increase }
        set_variable={ fct_dem_effect_multiplier=tmp_dem_effect }
        #########  ############
        custom_effect_tooltip=GRE_fct_effect_multiplier_change_shrt_title
        custom_effect_tooltip=GRE_fct_effect_multiplier_change_shrt_up_dem
        ###[Remove Days from Mission]###
        set_temp_variable={ tmpARD=days_mission_timeout@GRE_repub_upr }
        set_temp_variable_to_random= { var=percentage_days_lost min=0.01 max=0.2 }
        multiply_temp_variable={ tmpARD=percentage_days_lost }
        round_temp_variable=tmpARD
        set_temp_variable={ tmpDIS=tmpARD }
        multiply_temp_variable={ tmpARD=-1 }
        custom_effect_tooltip = mis_impacts_header
        set_temp_variable={ tmpMISS=1 }
        set_temp_variable={ tmpSIGN=1 }
        custom_effect_tooltip = mis_impact
        hidden_effect={ add_days_mission_timeout = { mission=GRE_repub_upr days=tmpARD }}
        ################################
        custom_effect_tooltip=GRE_fct_effect_multiplier_over_200_danger_tt
        custom_effect_tooltip=h352_dem_additional_days_lost_tt
        GRE_faction_refresh=yes
    }

    option={
        name=hellas.352.b
        trigger={ check_variable={ var=fct_dem value=40 compare=greater_than_or_equals }}

        add_political_power=25
        add_stability=0.025
        ###[BoP]###
        set_temp_variable={ tmpMOV=0.025 }
        fluctuate_bop_by_tmpMOV_tmpTT=yes
        ###[Increase Overall Effect Multiplier]###
        set_temp_variable_to_random={ var=tmp_mon_effect_increase min=6 max=14 }
        set_temp_variable={ tmp_mon_effect=fct_mon_effect_multiplier }
        add_to_temp_variable={ tmp_mon_effect=tmp_mon_effect_increase }
        set_variable={ fct_mon_effect_multiplier=tmp_mon_effect }
        clamp_variable={ var=fct_dem_effect_multiplier max=125 }
        #########  ############
        custom_effect_tooltip=GRE_fct_effect_multiplier_change_shrt_title
        custom_effect_tooltip=GRE_fct_effect_multiplier_change_shrt_up_mon
        custom_effect_tooltip=h352_clamp_dem_max
        #######################
        clr_country_flag=republicans_rebellious_initiated
    }
}

            }

                NOT = { has_country_flag = republican_uprising_utterly_crushed }
                NOT = { has_country_flag = dem_civilwar_started }

                NOT = { has_country_flag = com_civilwar_started }

                IEQ_TECH="[GRE.GetNextInfEq]"
                SEQ_TECH="[GRE.GetNextSupEq]"
            }
        }
        #clear_variable=gpcc_investment
    }

country_event = {
	id = hellas.501
	title = hellas.501.t
	desc = hellas.501.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_gre_allied_diplomacy

	is_triggered_only = yes
    
	option = {
		name = hellas.501.a #small investment

        set_temp_variable = { findX = FROM.id }
        set_temp_variable = { findY = -4 }
        fluctuate_favor_with_findX_by_findY=yes
        ##########################################################
        divide_temp_variable={ civ_chance?FROM.num_of_civilian_factories=FROM.num_of_factories }
        divide_temp_variable={ mil_chance?FROM.num_of_military_factories=FROM.num_of_factories }
        divide_temp_variable={ dck_chance?FROM.num_of_naval_factories=FROM.num_of_factories }
        set_temp_variable={ factory_gain_chance=35 }
        if={ limit={ check_variable={ FROM.num_of_factories>100 }} add_to_temp_variable={ factory_gain_chance=15 }}
        multiply_temp_variable={ civ_chance=factory_gain_chance }
        multiply_temp_variable={ mil_chance=factory_gain_chance }
        multiply_temp_variable={ dck_chance=factory_gain_chance }
        subtract_from_temp_variable={ misc_gain_chance?100=factory_gain_chance }
        divide_temp_variable={ infr_chance?misc_gain_chance=4 }
        divide_temp_variable={ anta_chance?misc_gain_chance=4 }
        divide_temp_variable={ airb_chance?misc_gain_chance=4 }
        divide_temp_variable={ fuel_chance?misc_gain_chance=4 }
        random_list={
            civ_chance={
                random_owned_controlled_state={ 
                    limit={ is_core_of=GRE free_building_slots={ building=industrial_complex size>1 include_locked=yes }}
                    add_building_construction={ type=industrial_complex level=1 instant_build=yes }
                }
            }
            mil_chance={
                random_owned_controlled_state={ 
                    limit={ is_core_of=GRE free_building_slots={ building=arms_factory size>1 include_locked=yes }}
                    add_building_construction={ type=arms_factory level=1 instant_build=yes }
                }
            }
            dck_chance={
                random_owned_controlled_state={ 
                    limit={ is_core_of=GRE free_building_slots={ building=dockyard size>1 include_locked=yes }}

                }
            }
            infr_chance={
                random_owned_controlled_state={ 
                    limit={ is_core_of=GRE free_building_slots={ building=infrastructure size>1 include_locked=yes }}
                    add_building_construction={ type=infrastructure level=1 instant_build=yes }
                }
            }
            anta_chance={
                random_owned_controlled_state={ 
                    limit={ is_core_of=GRE free_building_slots={ building=anti_air_building size>1 include_locked=yes }}
                    add_building_construction={ type=anti_air_building level=1 instant_build=yes }
                }
            }
            airb_chance={
                random_owned_controlled_state={ 
                    limit={ is_core_of=GRE free_building_slots={ building=air_base size>2 include_locked=yes }}
                    add_building_construction={ type=air_base level=2 instant_build=yes }
                }
            }
            fuel_chance={

                    limit={ is_core_of=GRE OR={ has_state_category=megalopolis has_state_category=metropolis } free_building_slots={ building=fuel_silo size>1 include_locked=yes }}

            }

                    else_if = { limit={ state_population_k<1200 } add_extra_state_shared_building_slots=3 }

                every_owned_state = {
                    if = { limit={ state_population_k<400 } add_extra_state_shared_building_slots=0 }
                    else_if = { limit={ state_population_k<800 } add_extra_state_shared_building_slots=1 }
                    else_if = { limit={ state_population_k<1200 } add_extra_state_shared_building_slots=2 }
                    else_if = { limit={ state_population_k<2000 } add_extra_state_shared_building_slots=3 }

                }
            }

        }
    }

news_event = {                                                                                  ### Italian Spring Offensive
	id = hellas.106
	title = hellas.106.t
	desc = hellas.106.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_italian_rise

	trigger = {
        original_tag = ITA
        has_war_with = GRE
        controls_state = 44
        date > 1941.3.8
    }

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = hellas.106.a

		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
        }
        
        swap_ideas = { 
            remove_idea = GRE_italian_ambition
            add_idea = GRE_italian_ambition_ultra_offensive
        }
        
        if = {
            limit = { 
                GRE = { has_completed_focus = GRE_prepare_spring_offensive }
            }
            add_timed_idea = {
                idea = ITA_spring_offensive
                days = 7
            }
        }
        else = {
            add_timed_idea = {
                idea = ITA_spring_offensive
                days = 30
            }
        }
        
        GRE = { 
            country_event = { id = hellenic_news.152 days = 0 } 
            set_country_flag = GRE_italian_spring_offensive_started
        }
        
    }
}

			}
            modifier = {
                factor = 0.5
                check_variable = { var = GER.favor@GRE value = 60 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
                check_variable = { var = GER.favor@GRE value = 80 compare = less_than }

		}

    }

country_event = {                                                                                  ### Greece managed to capilutate Bulgaria on time 
	id = hellas.113
	title = hellas.113.t
	desc = hellas.113.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_bulgarslayer

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {                                                                                      ## Annex if collaborative  
		name = hellas.113.a
        trigger = {
            check_variable = { var = BUL.favor@GRE value = 50 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
            has_collaboration = { target = BUL value > 0.45}
        }
        set_variable = { GRE.bulgarian_smackdown = 3 }
        if = {
            limit = {
                has_collaboration = { target = BUL value > 0.75}
            }
            annex_country = {
                target = BUL
                transfer_troops = yes
            }            
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = {
                has_collaboration = { target = BUL value > 0.45}
            }
            annex_country = {
                target = BUL
                transfer_troops = no
            }
        }
    }
    
    option = {                                                                                      ## Make it integrated puppet
		name = hellas.113.b
        trigger = {
            OR = {
                check_variable = { var = BUL.favor@GRE value = 50 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
                has_collaboration = { target = BUL value > 0}
            }
        }
        set_variable = { GRE.bulgarian_smackdown = 2 }
        hidden_effect = {
            puppet = BUL
            set_autonomy = {
                target = BUL
                autonomy_state = autonomy_integrated_puppet
            }
        }
    }
    
    option = {                                                                                      ## Keep as it is
		name = hellas.113.c
        set_variable = { GRE.bulgarian_smackdown = 1 }
    }
}

        trigger = { check_variable = { var = GRE.negotiations_willingness value = 0 compare = less_than_or_equals } }
    }
	desc = {                                                                                        
        text = hellas.114_accepted.desc
        trigger = { check_variable = { GRE.negotiations_willingness > 0 } }
    }
    desc = {                                                                                        
        text = hellas.114_rejected.desc
        trigger = { check_variable = { var = GRE.negotiations_willingness value = 0 compare = less_than_or_equals } }                                           
    }
	picture = GFX_report_event_tirana
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = no
	
    immediate = {
        if = {
            limit = { check_variable = { GRE.negotiations_willingness > 0 } }
            hidden_effect = {
                ##################[Land Acquisition]##################
                if = { limit = { check_variable = { tc_requested_dodecan = 1 } } if = { limit = { ENG = { controls_state = 164 } check_variable = { ENG.favor@GRE > 59 } } transfer_state = 164 } else = { transfer_state = 164 } }
                if = { limit = { check_variable = { tc_requested_albania = 1 } } transfer_state = 44 }
                else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { tc_requested_albania = 2 } } release_puppet_on_controlled = ALB }
                else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { tc_requested_albania = 3 } } release_on_controlled = ALB }
                if = { limit = { check_variable = { tc_requested_north_ep = 1 } } transfer_state = 805 }
                #####################[Reparations]####################
                if = { limit = { check_variable = { tc_requested_industrial = 1 } } ITA = { add_timed_idea = { idea = GRE_shackled_italian_industry_low days = 180 } } }
                else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { tc_requested_industrial = 2 } } ITA = { add_timed_idea = { idea = GRE_shackled_italian_industry_medium days = 180 } } }
                else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { tc_requested_industrial = 3 } } ITA = { add_timed_idea = { idea = GRE_shackled_italian_industry_high days = 180 } } }
                if = { limit = { check_variable = { tc_requested_equipment = 1 } } ITA = { transfer_units_fraction = { target = GRE stockpile_ratio = 0.1 size = 0 } } }
                else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { tc_requested_equipment = 2 } } ITA = { transfer_units_fraction = { target = GRE stockpile_ratio = 0.25 size = 0 } } }
                else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { tc_requested_equipment = 3 } } ITA = { transfer_units_fraction = { target = GRE stockpile_ratio = 0.50 size = 0 } } }
                if = { limit = { check_variable = { tc_requested_apology = 1 } } add_political_power = 500 }
                if = { limit = { check_variable = { tc_requested_campaign = 1 } } ITA = { set_country_flag = domestic_pacification_campaign } }
                if = { limit = { check_variable = { tc_requested_apology = 1 } } ITA = { add_political_power = -150 add_stability = -0.2 add_war_support = -0.2 } }
                #####################[Future Stability]####################
                if = { limit = { check_variable = { tc_requested_guarantees = 1 } } every_country = { limit = { is_in_faction_with = ITA } give_guarantee = GRE } set_global_flag = german_insurances_over_greece }
                if = { limit = { check_variable = { tc_requested_non_agg = 1 } } ITA = { diplomatic_relation = { country = GRE relation = non_aggression_pact active = yes } set_global_flag = grecoitalian_non_aggression set_variable = { grecoitalian_na_renewal = 6 } } }
                else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { tc_requested_non_agg = 2 } } ITA = { diplomatic_relation = { country = GRE relation = non_aggression_pact active = yes } set_global_flag = grecoitalian_non_aggression set_variable = { grecoitalian_na_renewal = 9 } } }
                else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { tc_requested_non_agg = 3 } } ITA = { diplomatic_relation = { country = GRE relation = non_aggression_pact active = yes } set_global_flag = grecoitalian_non_aggression set_variable = { grecoitalian_na_renewal = 12 } } }
                #####################[Self Limitations]####################
                if = { limit = { check_variable = { tc_offered_max_25 = 1 } } set_country_flag = tc_self_limitation_units set_variable = { self_limitation_units = 25 } }
                if = { limit = { check_variable = { tc_offered_not_to_join_factions = 1 } } set_rule = { can_join_factions = no } }
                if = { limit = { check_variable = { tc_offered_not_war_declaration = 1 } } set_rule = { can_not_declare_war = yes } }
                if = { limit = { check_variable = { tc_offered_not_volunteers = 1 } } set_rule = { can_send_volunteers = no } }
                ###################[Basic Stuff]######################
                set_country_flag = GRE_victor_in_a_war
                set_country_flag = GRE_victor_in_a_big_war
                add_political_power = 500
                add_stability = 0.5
                add_war_support = 0.5
                white_peace = ITA 
                news_event={ id=hellenic_news.154 }
                if={ limit={ has_dynamic_modifier={ modifier=GRE_the_army_war_dyn }} country_event={ id=hellas.798 }}
                if={ limit={ has_dynamic_modifier={ modifier=GRE_the_army_war_dyn }} country_event={ id=hellas.799 }}
                complete_national_focus = GRE_the_weaves_of_fate
                set_global_flag = GRE_grecoitalian_ended
                clr_global_flag = GRE_grecoitalian_start
                clear_variable = GRE.negotiations_willingness
                clr_country_flag = enable_willingness_gui
            }
        }
    }

	option = {
		name = hellas.114.a
        trigger = { check_variable = { GRE.negotiations_willingness = 0 } }
        effect_tooltip = {
            add_political_power = 500
            add_stability = 0.5
            add_war_support = 0.5
        }
    }
    option = {
		name = hellas.114.b
        trigger = { check_variable = { var = GRE.negotiations_willingness value = 0 compare = less_than } check_variable = { tc_first_time_proposal = 0 } check_variable = { tc_humiliated_mussolini = 0 } }
        set_variable = { tc_first_time_proposal = -1 }
        set_variable = { tc_description = 0 }
        set_variable = { tc_land_locked = 0 }
        set_variable = { tc_economic_locked = 0 }
        set_variable = { tc_future_locked = 0 }
        set_variable = { GRE.tc_tirana_conference_choices = 0 }
        hidden_effect = { GRE = { country_event = { id = hellas.111 days = 0 }  } }
    }
    option = {

        trigger = { check_variable = { var = GRE.negotiations_willingness value = 0 compare = less_than } }
        hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = enable_willingness_gui }

        hidden_effect = { GRE = { country_event = { id = hellas.1173 days = 0 } } }

    option = {                                                                                      ## RETRACT

        else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { mr_mussolini_fate = 3 } } add_to_variable = { mr_total_ratings = 20 } }
        set_variable = { mr_mussolini_fate = 0 }

country_event = {                                                                                  ### Metaxas Ribbentrop Pact Reply Event
	id = hellas.118
	title = {
        text = hellas.118_accepted.t
        trigger = { check_variable = { mr_success = 1 } }
    }
    title = {
        text = hellas.118_rejected.t
        trigger = { check_variable = { mr_success = 0 } }
    }
    desc = {
        text = hellas.118_accepted.desc
        trigger = { check_variable = { mr_success = 1 } }
    }
    desc = {
        text = hellas.118_rejected1.desc
        trigger = { check_variable = { mr_success = 0 } check_variable = { mr_total_attemps < 2 } }
    }
    desc = {
        text = hellas.118_rejected2.desc
        trigger = { check_variable = { mr_success = 0 } check_variable = { mr_total_attemps = 2 } }
    }
	picture = GFX_report_event_metaxas_hitler
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = no
	
    immediate = {
        hidden_effect = {
         ###[Calculate Success or Failure]###
            set_temp_variable = { multpl = 100 }                                            ### [Logic] 
            divide_temp_variable = { multpl = GRE.mr_negotiations_threshold }                 # Since the threshold is reduced based of inf/axal, we need to adjust the total rating to 100.
            set_temp_variable = { adjusted_total = GRE.mr_total_ratings }                     # Then we adjust the probabilities. Every point above 50 counts as 2. If we have >95, its 100%.
            multiply_temp_variable = { adjusted_total = multpl }
            subtract_from_temp_variable = { adjusted_total = 50 }
            multiply_temp_variable = { adjusted_total = 2 }
            clamp_temp_variable = {
                var = adjusted_total
                min = 0
                max = 100
            }
            if = { limit = { check_variable = { adjusted_total > 94.99 } } set_temp_variable = { adjusted_total = 100 } }
            round_temp_variable = adjusted_total
            set_temp_variable = { cnter_chance = 100 }
            subtract_from_temp_variable = { cnter_chance = adjusted_total }
            random_list = {
                #log = yes
                seed = random
                var:adjusted_total = { set_temp_variable = { mr_success = 1 } }
                var:cnter_chance = { set_temp_variable = { mr_success = 0 } }
            }
         ###[Success Effects]###
            if = {
                limit = { check_variable = { mr_success = 1 } }
                ###[Green Light for Naval Invasion]###
                GER = { set_rule = { can_not_declare_war = yes } }
                set_global_flag = Metaxas_Ribbentrop_Pact
            }
        }
    }

	option = {
		name = hellas.118.a
        effect_tooltip = {
            GER = { set_rule = { can_not_declare_war = yes } }
        }
        custom_effect_tooltip = mr_no_declaration_tt
        trigger = { check_variable = { mr_success = 1 } }
    }
    option = {
		name = hellas.118.b
        trigger = { check_variable = { mr_success = 0 } check_variable = { mr_total_attemps < 2 } }
        add_to_variable = { mr_total_attemps = 1 }
        hidden_effect = { GRE = { country_event = { id = hellas.117 days = 0 } } }
    }
    option = {
		name = hellas.118.c
        trigger = { check_variable = { mr_success = 0 } }
    }
}

country_event = {                                                                               ### Greece left Bulgarian border unmanned, make Bulgars declare war (mission -> ) 
	id = hellas.130
	title = hellas.130.t
	desc = hellas.130.desc

	trigger = {
        tag = GRE
        NOT = { has_global_flag = GRE_grecoitalian_ended }
        has_global_flag = GRE_grecoitalian_start
        OR = {
            ITA = { has_war_with = GRE }
            BUL = { is_in_faction_with = GER }
            BUL = { is_in_faction_with = ITA }
        }
        BUL = { 
            exists = yes
            NOT = { has_war_with = GRE } 
            OR = {
                NOT = { is_puppet_of = GRE }
                NOT = { is_subject_of = GRE }
            }
        }
        divisions_in_border_state = {
            type = infantry
            size < 3
            state = 940
            border_state = 212
        }     
        divisions_in_border_state = {
            type = infantry
            size < 1
            state = 731
            border_state = 212
        } 
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	#Give into Greece
	option = {
		name = hellas.130.a

        activate_mission = GRE_reman_bulgarian_line
    }
}
