country_event = {                                                                                                   ## Army buffs fade
	id = hellas.798
	title = hellas.798.t
	desc = hellas.798.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_greek_alb_failing_supply

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = hellas.798.a
        set_variable={ GRE_var_supply_consumption = 0 }
        set_variable={ GRE_var_winter_attr = 0 }
        set_variable={ GRE_var_cold_acc = 0 }
        if={
            limit={ check_variable={ GRE.leader_potency_drop_level=0 }}
            custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_officer_potency_drops_tt
            unit_leader_preparation_stats_fade=yes
            set_variable={ GRE.leader_potency_drop_level=1 }
        }
    }
}

country_event = {                                                                                                   ## Army buffs gone
	id = hellas.799
	title = hellas.799.t
	desc = hellas.799.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_greek_alb_march

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {                                                                            
		name = hellas.799.a
        
        remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GRE_the_army_war_dyn }
        if = {
            limit={ check_variable={ GRE.leader_potency_drop_level=1 }}
            custom_effect_tooltip=GRE_officer_potency_drops_tt
            unit_leader_preparation_stats_fade=yes
            set_variable={ GRE.leader_potency_drop_level=2 }
        }
    }
}

country_event = {                                                                                                   ### Big chain of events start here, during the next winter after the war has started (historically: 1942)
	id = hellas.800
	title = hellas.800.t
	desc = hellas.800.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_greek_triumph

    is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {                                                                                                          ## Open up negotiations
		name = hellas.800.a
        
        ITA = { faction_leader = { country_event = { id = hellas.801 days = 0 } } }                                     # This is obviously going to be the Germans, BUT you never know and always write code ticking most boxes that pop in ur head as scenarios.
    }
    
    option = {                                                                                                          ## Continue
		name = hellas.800.b

    }
    
    option = {                                                                                                          ## Speak with the British first
		name = hellas.800.c

    }
}

country_event = {                                                                                                   ### Enemy faction leader receives "yes" for negotiations
	id = hellas.801
	title = hellas.801.t
	desc = hellas.801.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_greek_triumph
	
    is_triggered_only = yes
    fire_only_once = yes

    immediate = {                                                                                                    ## What is going to happen next is collecting agreeableness from leader and faction members fighting Greece in the Greco-Italian war. States are 0,1,2,3 where 3 is max.
        hidden_effect = { collect_faction_member_agreeableness = yes }
    }
	
	option = {
		name = hellas.801.a
        ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
        GRE = { country_event = { id = hellas.802 days = 0 } }
    }
    
    option = {                                                                                                        # We break negotiations if human faction leader player is not willing.
		name = hellas.801.b
        ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
        #GRE = { country_event = { id = hellas.xxx days = 0 } }
    }
}

country_event = {                                                                                                   ### Enemy faction leader receives "yes" for negotiations
	id = hellas.802
	title = hellas.802.t
	desc = hellas.802.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_greek_triumph
	
    is_triggered_only = yes
    fire_only_once = no
	
	option = {                                                                                                       ## Greek player sees on screen the state of agreableness of the AI and decides to proceed.
		name = hellas.802.a
        trigger = {
            NOT = { has_country_flag = completed_demands_with_italy }
        }

        GRE = { country_event = { id = hellas.803 days = 0 } }                                                        # We will start by making demands out of the Italians.
    }
    
    option = {                                                                                                       ## Greek player sees on screen the state of agreableness of the AI and decides to proceed.
		name = hellas.802.b
        trigger = {
            NOT = { has_country_flag = completed_demands_with_bulgaria }
        }

        GRE = { country_event = { id = hellas.804 days = 0 } }                                                        # Bulgarian demands.
    }
    
    option = {                                                                                                       ## Greek player sees on screen the state of agreableness of the AI and decides to proceed.
		name = hellas.802.c
        trigger = {
            NOT = { has_country_flag = completed_demands_with_germany }
        }

        GRE = { country_event = { id = hellas.805 days = 0 } }                                                        # German demands.
    }
    
    option = {                                                                                                       ## Greek player sees on screen the state of agreableness of the AI and decides to proceed.
		name = hellas.802.d
        trigger = {
            has_country_flag = completed_demands_with_italy
            has_country_flag = completed_demands_with_bulgaria
            has_country_flag = completed_demands_with_germany
        }

        GRE = { country_event = { id = hellas.806 days = 0 } }                                                        # German demands.
    }
    
    option = {                                                                                                       ## Decides to keep fighting afterall.
		name = hellas.802.b
        ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
    }
}

country_event = {                                                                                                   ### Greek demands over the Italians
	id = hellas.803
	title = hellas.803.t
	desc = hellas.803.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_greek_triumph
	
    is_triggered_only = yes
    fire_only_once = yes
    
    immediate = { 
        hidden_effect = { 
            set_country_flag = completed_demands_with_italy 
            country_event = { id = hellas.802 days = 1 }
        }
    }
	
	option = {                                                                                                       ## Demand Albania / Northern Epirus / Dodecanese
		name = hellas.803.a
        trigger = { 
            check_variable = { var = ITA.nation_agreeableness_score value = 3 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
        }
        set_country_flag = ita_all_three_demanded
    }
    
    option = {                                                                                                       ## Northern Epirus / Dodecanese
		name = hellas.803.b
        trigger = { 
            check_variable = { var = ITA.nation_agreeableness_score value = 2 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
        }
        set_country_flag = ita_two_demanded
    }
    
    option = {                                                                                                       ## Northern Epirus
		name = hellas.803.c
        trigger = { 
            check_variable = { var = ITA.nation_agreeableness_score value = 1 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
        }
        set_country_flag = ita_ne_demanded
    }
    
    option = {                                                                                                       ## Dodecanese
		name = hellas.803.d
        trigger = { 
            check_variable = { var = ITA.nation_agreeableness_score value = 1 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
        }
        set_country_flag = ita_dod_demanded
    }
    
    option = {
		name = hellas.803.e
    }
}

country_event = {                                                                                                   ### Greek demands over the Italians
	id = hellas.804
	title = hellas.804.t
	desc = hellas.804.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_greek_triumph
	
    is_triggered_only = yes
    fire_only_once = yes
    
    immediate = { 
        hidden_effect = { 
            set_country_flag = completed_demands_with_bulgaria 
            country_event = { id = hellas.802 days = 1 }
        }
    }
	
	option = {                                                                                                       ## Take all their stockpile and disband their units
		name = hellas.804.a
        trigger = { 
            check_variable = { var = BUL.nation_agreeableness_score value = 3 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
        }
        set_country_flag = bul_stockpile_and_units_disbanded
    }
    
    option = {                                                                                                       ## Disband units + 50% of stockpile
		name = hellas.804.b
        trigger = { 
            check_variable = { var = BUL.nation_agreeableness_score value = 2 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
        }
        set_country_flag = bul_units_disbanded
    }
    
    option = {                                                                                                       ## Take all their stockpile, do not disband units
		name = hellas.804.c
        trigger = { 
            check_variable = { var = BUL.nation_agreeableness_score value = 2 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
        }
        set_country_flag = bul_stockpile
    }
    
    option = {
		name = hellas.804.d
    }    
}

country_event = {                                                                                                   ### PEACE ACHIEVED
	id = hellas.806
	title = hellas.806.t
	desc = hellas.806.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_greek_triumph
	
    
    is_triggered_only = yes
    fire_only_once = no
	
	option = {
		name = hellas.806.a
         
        every_country = {
            limit = { is_in_faction_with = ITA }
            white_peace = GRE
        }
        news_event = { id = hellenic_news.154 }
        complete_national_focus = GRE_the_weaves_of_fate
        complete_national_focus = GRE_glorious_struggle_in_triumph
        set_global_flag = GRE_grecoitalian_ended
        clr_global_flag = GRE_grecoitalian_start
        if = { 
            limit = { has_country_flag = ita_all_three_demanded }    
            GRE = { transfer_state = 44 }
            GRE = { transfer_state = 805 }   
            GRE = { transfer_state = 164 }    
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { has_country_flag = ita_two_demanded }
            GRE = { transfer_state = 805 }   
            GRE = { transfer_state = 164 }  
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { has_country_flag = ita_ne_demanded }
            GRE = { transfer_state = 805 }   
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { has_country_flag = ita_dod_demanded }  
            GRE = { transfer_state = 164 }  
        }
        if = {
            limit = { has_country_flag = bul_stockpile_and_units_disbanded }    
            BUL = { 
                #teleport_armies = { to_state = 48 } 
                delete_unit = {
                    state = 48
                    disband = yes
                }
                transfer_units_fraction= {
                    target = GRE
                    size = 1
                    stockpile_ratio = 1
                    army_ratio = 1
                    navy_ratio = 1
                    air_ratio = 1
                    keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
                        always = yes
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { has_country_flag = bul_stockpile }
            BUL = {
                transfer_units_fraction= {
                    target = GRE
                    size = 1
                    stockpile_ratio = 1
                    army_ratio = 0
                    navy_ratio = 0
                    air_ratio = 0
                    keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
                        always = yes
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        else_if = {
            limit = { has_country_flag = bul_units_disbanded }
            BUL = { 
                #teleport_armies = { to_state = 48 } 
                delete_unit = { 
                    state = 48
                    disband = yes
                }
                transfer_units_fraction= {
                    target = GRE
                    size = 0
                    stockpile_ratio = 0.5
                    army_ratio = 0
                    navy_ratio = 0
                    air_ratio = 0
                    keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
                        always = yes
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }
}

	fire_only_once = yes
    
	
	option = {                                                                            
		name = hellas.9995.a
        
        GRE_king_george = { remove_country_leader_role = { ideology = despotism } }
        promote_character = GRE_emmanouil_tsouderos

            limit = {
                NOT = { has_completed_focus = GRE_dreams_of_a_grand_coalition } 
            }
            set_party_name = { 
                ideology = neutrality
                long_name = GRE_neutrality_party
                name = GRE_neutrality_party
            }
        }
    }
}


country_event = {                                                                                   ## Tsolakoglou's Capitulation                                                                          
	id = hellas.1000
	title = hellas.1000.t
	desc = hellas.1000.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_tsolak_capit

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes
	
    immediate = {
        hidden_effect = {
            set_variable = { treaty_signed_date = global.date }
            retire_character = GRE_georgios_tsolakoglou
            if = {
                limit = { has_country_flag = tsolakoglou_initiative }
                every_state = {                                                                             ##disband armies due to capitulation
                        limit = {
                            OR = {
                                is_owned_by = GRE
                                is_controlled_by = GRE
                            }
                            NOT = { state = 182 }                                                            # This doesn't apply for Sterea Ellada / Attika / Peloponnese / Crete / Nisia Aegeou
                            NOT = { state = 47  }
                            NOT = { state = 186 }
                            NOT = { state = 935 }
                            NOT = { state = 187 }
                            NOT = { state = 942 }
                        }
                        GRE = {
                            delete_unit = { 
                                state = PREV
                                disband = yes
                            }
                        }
                    }
                GRE = {                                                                                     ##a n extra check if u are stuck in half of albania
                    delete_unit = {
                        state = 44
                        disband = yes
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }
    
	option = {                                                                                                                                                         
		name = hellas.1000.a

        clear_variable = treaty_signed_date
    }
}

country_event = {
	id = hellas.1003
	title = hellas.1003.t
	desc = hellas.1003.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_hellenic_state

	is_triggered_only = yes 
    
	fire_only_once = yes
    
    immediate = {
        hidden_effect = {
            set_global_flag = weekly_favor_mechanic_frozen
            set_global_flag = GRE_hellenic_state_formed
            set_global_flag = GRE_grecoitalian_ended
            set_global_flag = GRE_crete_still_holding
            clr_global_flag = GRE_grecoitalian_start
            create_dynamic_country = {
                original_tag = GRE
                save_global_event_target_as = hellenic_state
                #############################[Preliminary State Transfer]############################
                every_state = {
                    limit = {
                        is_owned_by = GRE
                        NOT = { state = 182 }
                    }
                    event_target:hellenic_state = { transfer_state = PREV }
                }
                GER = { transfer_state = 47 transfer_state = 939 }                                                                   # TEMPORARILY TO NAVAL INVADE CRETE (doesn't work otherwise)
                set_capital = { state = 47 }
                add_to_array = { global.axis_occupiers=GER.id }
                add_to_array = { global.axis_occupiers=ITA.id }
                #############################[Setup Occupation Zones]############################
                941 = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GRE_german_occupation_zone } }
                731 = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GRE_german_occupation_zone } }
                939 = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GRE_german_occupation_zone } }
                938 = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GRE_german_occupation_zone } }
                47 = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GRE_german_occupation_zone } }
                187 = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GRE_german_occupation_zone } }
                935 = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GRE_italian_occupation_zone } }
                936 = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GRE_italian_occupation_zone } }
                937 = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GRE_italian_occupation_zone } }
                186 = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GRE_italian_occupation_zone } }
                185 = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GRE_italian_occupation_zone } } 
                942 = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GRE_italian_occupation_zone } } 
                #######################[Bulgarian Direct Annexations (Historical)]###############
                if = {                                                                                                              # If Bulgaria is alive, in Axis and historical stuff should happen.
                    limit = {
                        BUL = {
                            exists = yes
                            OR = {
                                is_in_faction_with = GER
                                is_in_faction_with = ITA
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    731 = { clr_state_flag = BUL_historical_bulgarian_claim_flag }
                    731 = { clr_state_flag = BUL_bulgarian_claim_warranted_flag }
                    731 = { remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = bulgarian_territorial_expansion_arranged } }
                    939 = { clr_state_flag = BUL_historical_bulgarian_claim_flag }
                    939 = { clr_state_flag = BUL_bulgarian_claim_warranted_flag }
                    939 = { remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = bulgarian_territorial_expansion_arranged } }
                    941 = { clr_state_flag = BUL_historical_bulgarian_claim_flag }
                    941 = { clr_state_flag = BUL_bulgarian_claim_warranted_flag }
                    941 = { remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = bulgarian_territorial_expansion_arranged } }
                    184 = { BUL = { transfer_state = PREV } }
                    940 = { BUL = { transfer_state = PREV } }
                    add_to_array = { global.axis_occupiers=BUL.id }
                }
                else = {
                    184 = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GRE_italian_occupation_zone } }                                      # Italians take control of their portion, as this would have happened historically since the Germans only took strategic regions and Italians the mass of land.
                    940 = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GRE_italian_occupation_zone } } 
                }
                ################################[Set HS Rules]###################################
                set_rule = { 
                    can_join_factions = no 
                    can_create_factions = no
                    can_not_declare_war = yes
                    can_send_volunteers = no
                }
                ################################[Political Setting]###################################
                set_politics = { ruling_party = fascism elections_allowed = no }
                set_popularities = { democratic = 15 fascism = 50 neutrality = 20 communism = 15 }
                set_cosmetic_tag = GRE_HELLENIC_STATE_fascism
                GRE = {                                                                     ## Disband Units in Aegean Islands and mainland Greece
                    delete_unit = {state = 935 disband = yes}
                    delete_unit = {state = 47 disband = yes}
                    delete_unit = {state = 186 disband = yes}
                    delete_unit = {state = 187 disband = yes}
                    delete_unit = {state = 942 disband = yes}
                    set_temp_variable = { convoy_num = GRE.convoys_secured }
                    multiply_temp_variable = { convoy_num = -1 }
                    add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
                        type = convoy_1
                        amount = convoy_num
                        producer = GRE
                    }
                    transfer_units_fraction = {                                             ## Germany takes 75% of stockpile from virtually SURRENDERED troops
                        target = GER                                                         # This is why evacuated divisions will retain equipment, while disbanded (see above) will put eq to stockpile.
                        size = 0                                                             # So basically the 25% left is what you """evacuated""" to Crete.
                        stockpile_ratio = 0.75
                        army_ratio = 0
                        navy_ratio = 0.0
                        air_ratio = 0.0
                        keep_unit_leaders_trigger = { always = yes }
                    }
                }
                ################################[Characters/Technologies/Ideas/Focuses]###################################
                HS_split_characters_to_respective_nations=yes
                promote_character = GRE_georgios_tsolakoglou
                if = { limit = { GRE = { has_country_flag = archbishop_damaskinos_elected } } event_target:hellenic_state = { complete_national_focus = oust_chrysanthus_for_damaskinos } }
                inherit_technology = GRE
                set_research_slots = 0
                add_ideas = HS_ind_shackles_4
                add_ideas = HS_tripple_occupation
                add_ideas = HS_occupation_costs
                add_ideas = HS_german_plundering
                add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier=HS_death }
                #add_ideas = HS_death
                if = {
                    limit = { GRE = { has_completed_focus = GRE_dreams_of_a_grand_coalition } }
                    add_ideas = HS_spirit_of_grand_coalition
                }
                load_focus_tree = hellenic_state_focus
                GRE = { GR_HS_split_ideas = yes }
                #GER = { puppet = event_target:hellenic_state }
                complete_national_focus = glorious_struggle_in_vain
                complete_national_focus = hellenic_state
                complete_national_focus = appoint_tsolakoglou
            }
            every_country = {
                limit = { is_in_faction_with = GER }
                diplomatic_relation = {
                    country = event_target:hellenic_state
                    relation = non_aggression_pact
                    active = yes
                }
                diplomatic_relation = {
                    country = event_target:hellenic_state
                    relation = military_access
                    active = yes
                }
            }
            GER = {
                add_timed_idea = { idea = GRE_german_ambition_crete days = 60 }
                diplomatic_relation = {
                    country = event_target:hellenic_state
                    relation = guarantee
                    active = yes
                }
                remove_ideas = GRE_german_ambition
            }
            ITA = {
                diplomatic_relation = {
                    country = event_target:hellenic_state
                    relation = guarantee
                    active = yes
                }
            }
            HS_calculate_initial_anger_level = yes
            HS_set_up_occupation_zones = yes
            HS_set_up_areas_of_interest_arrays = yes
            HS_calculate_factories_in_occupation_zones = yes
            HS_flag_states = yes 
            HS_shut_down_the_games_resistance_mechanic_in_states = yes
            #######[Resource Rights for Sterea/Pel. go to the Reich]######
            ITA = { give_resource_rights = { receiver = GER state = 935 } }
            ITA = { give_resource_rights = { receiver = GER state = 186 } }
            ##############################################################
            GRE = { country_event = { id = hellas.1004 days = 10 } }
        }
    }
	
	option = { name = hellas.1003.a }
}

state_event = {                                                                                   ## Plunder of State Event (STATE)                                                    
	id = hellas.1016
	title = hellas.1016.t
	desc = hellas.1016.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_hs_plunder

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = no
    
    immediate = {
        hidden_effect = { 
            HS_GAR_EVNT_outcome_calculation = yes
            random_list = {
                seed=random
                var:case0 = {
                    set_variable = { plun_state_fam = 1 }
                    set_variable = { plun_state_agi = 0.04 }
                    set_variable = { plun_state_and = 8 }
                    set_variable = { plun_state_and_per = 0 }
                    set_variable = { plun_severity=1 }
                }
                var:case1 = {
                    set_variable = { plun_state_fam = 1 }
                    set_variable = { plun_state_agi = 0.08 }
                    set_variable = { plun_state_and = 10 }
                    set_variable = { plun_state_and_per = 0 }
                    set_variable = { plun_severity=2 }
                }
                var:case2 = {
                    set_variable = { plun_state_fam = 1 }
                    set_variable = { plun_state_agi = 0.12 }
                    set_variable = { plun_state_and = 12 }
                    set_variable = { plun_state_and_per = 0 }
                    set_variable = { plun_severity=3 }
                }
                var:case3 = {
                    set_variable = { plun_state_fam = 1 }
                    set_variable = { plun_state_agi = 0.14 }
                    set_variable = { plun_state_and = 16 }
                    set_variable = { plun_state_and_per = 0 }
                    set_variable = { plun_severity=4 }
                }
                var:case4 = {
                    set_variable = { plun_state_fam = 2 }
                    set_variable = { plun_state_agi = 0.16 }
                    set_variable = { plun_state_and = 18 }
                    set_variable = { plun_state_and_per = 0.05 }
                    set_variable = { plun_severity=5 }
                }
                var:case5 = {

                    set_variable = { plun_state_and = 20 }
                    set_variable = { plun_state_and_per = 0.10 }
                    set_variable = { plun_severity=6 }

                    set_variable = { plun_state_and = 22 }
                    set_variable = { plun_state_and_per = 0.15 }

            add_dynamic_modifier={ modifier=plundered_state days=30 }

state_event = {                                                                                   ## Deploys Andartes
	id = hellas.1600
	title = hellas.1600.t
	desc = hellas.1600.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_greek_hs_hungry_kids

    timeout_days=0
    is_triggered_only=yes
	fire_only_once = no
    hidden = yes
    
    immediate = {
        hidden_effect = {
            add_to_variable = { THIS.andartes=th }
            set_temp_variable = { tmp=combatant_percentage }
            multiply_temp_variable = { tmp=th }
            add_to_variable = { THIS.available_combatants=tmp }
            set_temp_variable = { tmp=noncombatant_percentage }
            multiply_temp_variable = { tmp=th }
            add_to_variable = { THIS.available_noncombatants=tmp }
            set_temp_variable = { tmp=reservist_percentage }
            multiply_temp_variable = { tmp=th }
            add_to_variable = { THIS.available_reservists=tmp }
            clr_state_flag = state_deploying_recalling
            clear_variable = th
        }
    }

    option = { name=hellas.1600.a ai_chance={ base=100 } }
}

state_event = {                                                                                   ## Recalls Andartes
	id = hellas.1601
	title = hellas.1601.t
	desc = hellas.1601.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_greek_hs_hungry_kids

    timeout_days=1
    is_triggered_only=yes
	fire_only_once = no
    hidden = yes

            add_to_variable = { GRE.andartes_pool=th }

            clear_variable = th
        }
    }
    
    option = { name=hellas.1601.a ai_chance={ base=100 } }

state_event = {                                                                                   ## Restructures Troops in State
	id = hellas.1602
	title = hellas.1602.t
	desc = hellas.1602.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_greek_hs_hungry_kids

    timeout_days=1
    is_triggered_only=yes
	fire_only_once = no
    hidden = yes
    
    immediate = {
        hidden_effect = {
            ##############
            #[Combatants]#
            ##############
            set_temp_variable={ x=gui_combatant_percentage }
            multiply_temp_variable={ x=THIS.andartes }
            set_variable={ available_combatants=x }
            set_variable={ combatant_percentage=gui_combatant_percentage }
            ##################
            #[Non-Combatants]#
            ##################
            set_temp_variable={ x=gui_noncombatant_percentage }
            multiply_temp_variable={ x=THIS.andartes }
            if = { 
                limit = {                                                                                       # We have enough available non combatants.
                    set_temp_variable={ xx=gui_noncombatant_percentage }
                    multiply_temp_variable={ xx=THIS.andartes }
                    check_variable={ var=xx value=THIS.allocated_noncombatants compare=greater_than_or_equals }
                }
                subtract_from_temp_variable={ x=THIS.allocated_noncombatants }
            }
            else ={ reset_entire_state_unarmed_resistance=yes }                                                 # We do not have enough and need to take from allocated.
            set_variable={ available_noncombatants=x }
            set_variable={ noncombatant_percentage=gui_noncombatant_percentage }
            ##############
            #[Reservists]#
            ##############
            set_temp_variable={ x=gui_reservist_percentage }
            multiply_temp_variable={ x=THIS.andartes }
            set_variable={ available_reservists=x }
            set_variable={ reservist_percentage=gui_reservist_percentage }
            clr_state_flag = state_restructuring_forces
        }
    }

    option = { name=hellas.1602.a ai_chance={ base=100 } }
}

state_event = {                                                                                   ## Adds/Removes Equipment
	id = hellas.1603
	title = hellas.1603.t
	desc = hellas.1603.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_greek_hs_hungry_kids

    timeout_days=1
    is_triggered_only=yes
	fire_only_once = no
    hidden = yes
    
    immediate = {
        hidden_effect = {
            if = {
                limit = { has_state_flag = { flag=state_redeploying_equipment value=1 } }
                add_to_variable={ infeq=gui_infeq }
                add_to_variable={ supeq=gui_supeq }
                add_to_variable={ arteq=gui_arteq }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = { has_state_flag = { flag=state_redeploying_equipment value=2 } }
                add_to_variable={ GRE.andartes_infeq_reserve=gui_infeq }
                add_to_variable={ GRE.andartes_supeq_reserve=gui_supeq }
                add_to_variable={ GRE.andartes_arteq_reserve=gui_arteq }
            }
            clear_variable = gui_infeq
            clear_variable = gui_supeq
            clear_variable = gui_arteq
            clr_state_flag = state_redeploying_equipment
        }
    }
    
    option = { name=hellas.1603.a ai_chance={ base=100 } }
}

            GRE = { has_completed_focus = GRE_crete_falls }
        }
    }

    #}

        }
    }

        GER = { set_province_controller = 4109 }
        GER = { set_province_controller = 11965 }

            limit = { GRE = { has_completed_focus = GRE_crete_falls } }
            GRE = { transfer_state = 270 }
            event_target:hellenic_state = { transfer_state = 182 }
            GER = { set_province_controller = 12058 }
            GER = { set_province_controller = 1164 }
            GER = { set_province_controller = 9940 }
            GER = { set_province_controller = 4170 }
            add_to_array = { global.greek_occupied_states_all = 182 }
            add_to_array = { global.german_occupied_states = 182 }
            182 = { 
                add_resistance = 9 
                #add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = unyielding_greeks_angered }
                add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GRE_german_occupation_zone }
            }
            HS_calculate_factories_in_occupation_zones = yes
            country_event = { id = hellas.1007 days = 0 }
        }
        else = {
            country_event = { id = hellas.1006 days = 0 }
        }
    }
}
